## REASONSTORESEARCH

Like the vampiresofthe Worldof Darknesshe styles of magic in Blood Sacrifice are has ed on blend of foilre and fantasy -the legends and fiction of rhesourceculruresas wellastheiractual occult bcliefs. This reinforces rheillusion thr the Worldof Darknesscould bca hiddensidetoourteal world. More importantly, this gives you moregame material than we could ever publish Libruries and bookstoreshold treasuries of lore everything from collections of follktalesto scholarly anthropo Iogical sudiesthat can inspiremore Paths rialscharcters an sries

Remember thongl, that blood magic never preciscly imitates the for msof mortal occult or religious beliefs. don't feel too bound byrealism (adodgy concept for a game-about vampires）. Filter the myths and legends through the vampirie condition and the rules for Thaumaturgy to make somerhing new thar works with in you r game. Nahuallorl tend to mistrust vampires who do not share their mortal ancestry. Students of Wanga generally must devote the mselves toane of the Afro-Caribbean teligions. Sadhana mastersreputedly teach their art only to fellow undead brahmins. The Followersof Setcarelessforancesry than membersof many clons, but many will insist that would-bestudents of theirsorcery also devote the mselves to the Dark God. Anoutsidermay have to pass grueling tests of loyalty and devotion from a prospective mentor... ot else perpetrate an exceedingly dangerous fraud. Weurge playersand Storytellersto viewtheserestrictions asopportunities The search for magictuition, lore and ingredentscanjustify all sorts of stories. do esswash bucklingadventure-"Indiann Jones By Night—appcal toyou?Search for that lost temple or tomb. Do you prefer Creepy, Lovecraftian horror full of hideous secrets and Slimy Unspeakables？What luck. a reclusive vampire avant ina decaying backwoods village s said toknowthe ritualyouseek... and what anodd staruette he keepson his mantelpiece, lf you enjoy razor-edged intrigue. the chal lenge of opposed mentors should provide plenty of opportunities. Players can certainly take heir fill of er sonal horror as theircharactersleatmjust how far they will go for the sake of magical power. ## the CHALLENGEFROMBEYOND

The stylesof Thaumaturgy described in Blood Sorcery come from regions outside the"developed world that most players and characters know. As Western vam piresmcer theircounterparts in (and from}other lands. they encounterunfamiliar bloodmagic aswell. Even in the Westem world, the Tremere now face a minar (but growing)challenge to. their long-assumed monopoly on Thaumarrgy for centuries in the Camarillaa vampire who sought sorcerou5 aid bad to pay what ever price the local Tremere chargedandsmile. the Tremere ant had the Sabbat over a barrel in much the same way. Upheavals in both sects and among independent clans have broken that monopoly. The destruction of the Tremere antitrbu for ces the Sabbat toshopforaltermative magical resources. The civil war among the Assamites has launched a dinspora of theirbloodmagicians who petition both the Sabbat and Camarilla for protection. The Fol lowers of Ser vend their ancient occult prowess for their own obscure reasons. for eign princes court the blood brahmins just as mortalcorporations recruit computer programmers from India. In bothfearand fascination, the Tremereseck tomaster the secretartsoftheseotherthaumaturges. Longrestrictedto Europe and itscolonies, Clan Tremerenowseeksto expand its base. Globaliration is the new buzzword around the chantries. Everyonecleisdoingit, and the ever-competitive Tremere vow not to be leftbehind. Other Tremere expand their clan beyond its European roots more directly. by Embracing childer from amongtheseforeignpopulations, from Mexicancranderos to Indianholy men. Suchchilderbringan insider'sviewof their culture's magical traditions. The Tremere hope they can adapt native spells and conjurations just as the clan's founders adapted the Hermetic magic of medieval Europe. Thus will Clan Tremere assemble and synthesize all the magic in the world-or so they hope. In Africa and India, the Middle East and Central America, Ttemere savants ponder obscure clues with in ancient myths and excavate long-lost temples and tombs. Srudents kneel beforeundead sages, begging tolearn thcir mystic lore. and cunning clders weave vicious schemes to caprure those same sagesand extract secrets through torture. Some among the Tremere do ubtthisworld-spanning program. The for eign Thaumaturgy may be too, well, for eign. To learn another culture's magic, Tremere studentsfind they must learn and accept that culture'sbeliefs. the n, how ever... are they still Tremere Can the clan's elders trust the m?In seeking to encompass all blood sorcery with in itself，will Clan Tremere shatter itself beyond hope of reunion? ## BLOODSACRIFICE

When European scholars rediscovered Greek and Roman learningin the later Middle Ages, the yrecovered the ancients'astrology, mysticism and magic-chieflythe

Many impediments to learning non-Western Thaumaturgy boil do wn to religion. The Tremere clan culrure is not veryreligous. Sinceancienttimeshe West has denigrated and demonized magic. The Romans, so promiscuously tolerant of for eign religions, frequently launched waves of suppression against astrologers, for tune-tellers and all sorts of magicians. The Jewish Law likewisc condemned all sorcery except the mystical Kabbalah. Christianity inherited a suspicion of magic from bothsources. St. Augustineof Hippodeclared that an mighty for ged an implicit pact with Satan. Corps Hermeticonalong with Greco-Roman law. medicine, mathandrhetoric. Scholars pursued this occult lore at their peril. Pioneering Hermetics adopted avariety of do dgesto for estall the inquisitor. Some wrapped their spellsinprayer, and proclaimed that all magicworked by the sufferance of God. Others denied the mystical aspect of their spells, descrbing them as "natural magicthar cxploited subtleforcesof the planets, the elemenrsand the human spirit. The founders of Clan Tremere came from this culture. Both as mortals and vampires, they saw their magic as a practical craft with no religious implications. Apractical, diligent Tremeremust make asignificant conceptual leaptoleam the for ms of sorcery described in Blood Sacrifice. Eachmagical tradition intertwineswith are ligious tradition. A student who says, Nevermind the sermon. justteachme how tocastthespelldoesnotlearn much. A bokkor or brahmin believes his magic works because of his connectionto the divine. Hecould nomore divorce his magic from hisfaith than he could divorce the right side of his body from his left. Not every culrure separatesand opposesmagicandrel gion Egpanpries Hindubranndms combine the roles of priest and magician. Some anthropolo gists say that, A priest has a congregation; a magician has a clientele. Many occult practitioners have boch. Some Tremere do make that leap. they leamtobelieve inthedivinepowerbehindthebloodsorcery. not all of them retum to theirclanto explain what they have leamed. ## GAMEMECHANICS

Tremere paths generally do not require any material ingredient to operate. The vampire might whisper a few magic words to herself or trace a brief gesture to aid her concentration. Some of the non-Hermeticpaths, how ever, involve a small amulet or othermaterial component to trigger or direct the magic. All the se divergent styles of Thaumaturgy consis of pathsand rituals, just likethe Hermetic Thaumaturgyofthe Tremerndostobyhsamelesll that ugy derivesfrom the supermatural powerwithinvampiric vitac. Schoolsof bloodmagic holddifferentbeliefs about how to evoke and shape that intrinsicmagic, how ever, and those beliefsexplain their variations inmagical style and content. Hermetic Thaumaturgy uses a will power roll for all path powers this reflects the systematic and homogeneous nature of the Tremeresmagic Otherformsof Thaumaturgy mayusea different roll for eachpath, generallyan Atribute +Ability roll. Everyritualcallsforan Intelligence+Occultoll, but the cultural milieus that underlie styles of Thaumarurgy make differentassumptions about what Oecultmeams. AHemetic magus Santerane and a Hindusapossessvery differentbodies of esotericknowledge and ritual practice but the Storyteller Systemfiles them all under the blanket labelof Occult Playersmaywanttonote the sedifferences on the character'srecord sheet by addinga word to"Oecult": thus"Occult. Egyptian"or"Ocult. Wanga"Charctes who have Occult 4or higher can treat this as a specialry. ## LEARNINGTIMES

Before the Egyptians conceived of Amenti, how evet the ybelievedinagrimmerunderworldwhichtheyrerained for the dead who failed the test of Osris The Egyptians believed that after it sailedacrossthe sky curing the day, the boat of Ra sailedunder the Eanh through the cavems f Duat, the River of Death. ## MESOPOTAMIANSTATERELIGION

Some tine between the 1Oth and 6th centuries BC the prophet Zarathustra, or Zoroaster, radically reshaped the Magian religion. Zoroastrianism demores Mithra toa yaata, one of the second rnk of spiritsafter the aesha spenas(immortalholy ones"）who personify virtues, and Ahura Mada("Lord Wisdom), the supremedeiryof Light and Good. Anga Mayu ot Aman, the spirit of Evil opposed Ahra Mazda from the heginning of timeuntilits destinedend. Zorcastrian warship continues to center on fire, asrhe earthly symbol of Aura Mada's lighr. Holy books called the Zend-Avesta and the Giathas preserve Zoroastrian do ctrine.
